The\n * option is European, exercised only on the exercise date.\n * <p>\n * For example, a call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange is the option to perform a foreign exchange on the expiry\n * option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n Pricer Classes (modules/pricer/)\\n\\nThe project contains two pricing model variants with Product and Trade tier implementations:\\n\\n**Black Model Variant:**\\n- **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java): Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOption using the Black (lognormal) model. Uses DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer for underlying FX pricing and BlackFormulaRepository for option calculations.\\n\\n- **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java): Extends Black pricing to the trade level, incorporating premium adjustments.\\n\\n**Vanna-Volga Model Variant:**\\n- **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java): Implements the Vanna-Volga pricing methodology, which adjusts Black prices for smile effects using three market instruments (ATM, Risk Reversal, Butterfly).\\n\\n- **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java): Trade-level wrapper for Vanna-Volga pricing with premium handling.\\n\\n### 3. Measure Calculation Classes (modules/measure/)\\n\\nFour calculation classes wire the pricing layer to the calculation engine:\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations.java): Multi-scenario measure calculations aggregating Black and Vanna-Volga pricers. Contains methods for PV, Greeks, and other risk measures across scenario arrays.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java): Enumeration defining the pricing methodology selection (Black vs Vanna-Volga).\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction.java): Integration point with the calculation engine, dispatching trades to appropriate measure calculations.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations.java): Single-scenario trade-level measure calculations.\\n\\n### 4. Dependency Reference: FxSingleBarrierOption\\n\\n- **FxSingleBarrierOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxSingleBarrierOption.java): A barrier option type that embeds FxVanillaOption as a core dependency. The class contains a property `underlyingOption` of type FxVanillaOption, creating a composition relationship where a single barrier option wraps a vanilla option with additional barrier and rebate specifications.\\n\\n### Type Resolution Chain\\n\\nThe type hierarchy follows a resolution pattern: `FxVanillaOption` → (via resolve()) → `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` and `FxVanillaOptionTrade` → (via resolve()) → `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade`. This two-tier architecture separates contract specification from pricing-ready resolved forms, enabling efficient caching and batch processing of pricing requests.\\n\\n### Architectural Notes\\n\\n1. **Module Organization**: Clear separation of concerns across product (domain), pricer (computation), measure (integration), and loader (I/O) modules\\n2. **Pricing Model Flexibility**: Support for both Black (simple) and Vanna-Volga (smile-aware) methodologies through parallel class hierarchies\\n3. **Volatility Support**: Pricers leverage BlackFxOptionVolatilities and related surface classes for volatility term structures and smile dynamics\\n4. **Integration Pattern**: The calculation function pattern delegates pricing decisions based on selected method (FxVanillaOptionMethod)\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
